NATIONAL INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY KURUKSHETRA (ACADEMTC SEC No. Acad./OEl23-241 I Aqcl July 31 ,2024 NQTTFTCATTOJ.I This is in continuation to provisional allotment of Open Elective courses for B.Tech. Sth semester dated 29.07.2024 uploaded on the lnstitute website for A.Y. 2024-25. The Open Elective course have been finally allotted to the students of B.Tech. programs of Sth semester on the basis of choices, semester performance up to 3'd semester and discrepancy, if any, pointed out by the students. The list of students finally allotted Open Elective course and the Provisional Roll Sheet of Open Elective B.Tech. Sth semester is uploaded on the institute website under---Academic--- Roll Sheet---B.Tech. Sth Semester. ffir Facult Copy to: 1. AR to Director for kind information of the Hon'ble Director 2.
